<section id="custom_html-4" class="widget_text widget widget_custom_html"><div class="widget_text widget-wrap"><div class="textwidget custom-html-widget">I’m an American who’s lived in Italy for over 40 years, raising my family here and building a life rooted in food, travel, and culture. Through my blog, podcast, newsletter, and small-group trips, I share Italian stories, recipes, and practical travel insight shaped by real experience.
<br>
<br>
Cook with me, explore Italy beyond the obvious, meet local creators, and discover the country as it’s lived every day — at the table, on the road, and behind the scenes.
<br>
<br>
